      <svg class="icon site_header__hamburger" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
       <use href="/public/img/icons/jg-icons.2b416b55e07b4a6842d5f02c75f7b29a.spritesheet.svg#icon-ui-hamburger" xlink:href="/public/img/icons/jg-icons.2b416b55e07b4a6842d5f02c75f7b29a.spritesheet.svg#icon-ui-hamburger" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink">

    <script>
     (function() {
	    var site_header = document.querySelector('.site_header'),
			site_search = site_header.querySelector('.site_search'),
			sections    = site_header.querySelector('.site_nav__sections'),

			mega_menu   = site_header.querySelectorAll('.mega_menu'),
			mega_items,

			mega_menu_section_nav = sections.querySelectorAll('.mega_menu__section_nav_item'),
			current_section_item;

			// Toggle site header light/dark mode on hovering site nav
			if( site_header.classList.contains('site_header--transparent') ) {
				mega_items = sections.querySelectorAll('.dropdown__trigger');

				mega_items.forEach(function(mega_item) {
					mega_item.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(event) {
						site_header.classList.add('site_header--transparent-off');
						site_search.classList.remove('site_search--dark');
					});
					mega_item.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(event) {
						site_header.classList.remove('site_header--transparent-off');
						site_search.classList.add('site_search--dark');
					});
				});
			}

			// On mega menu section nav item hover, if item doesn't have sub-sections, show previous item's menu
			mega_menu_section_nav.forEach(function(nav_item) {
				nav_item.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(event) {
					if( !this.classList.contains('mega_menu__section_nav_item--has-subs') ) {
						var body_panel = current_section_item.querySelector('.mega_menu__body_panel');

						if( body_panel )
							body_panel.style.display = 'flex';
					}
					else {
						current_section_item = this;
					}
				});

				nav_item.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(event) {
					if( !this.classList.contains('mega_menu__section_nav_item--has-subs') ) {
						var body_panel = current_section_item.querySelector('.mega_menu__body_panel');

						if( body_panel )
							body_panel.style.display = "";
					}
				});
			});
	})();
    </script>
